font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Vijay is considered a\nloser by society. &nbsp;&nbsp;He is a fine poet who thirsts for recognition\nand fame.&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">His poems are rejected by\nall publishers, as they are too stark and full of melancholy. </span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">His brothers torment him\nas he cannot bring bread on the table. &nbsp;They\nsell his collection of poems for the worth of the scrap paper it is written on.&nbsp; <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">His college girlfriend,\nMeena , though in love with him, &nbsp;is\nmaterialistic and marries a rich publisher for financial security, &nbsp;breaking Vijay\u2019s heart.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Vijay realizes that this\nmaterialistic world &nbsp;is only for &nbsp;selfish and opportunistic people. &nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<br /></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Ghosh hires Vijay to dig out the possibly sordid past of\nhis wife Meena.<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">In this world of\nselfish people, a golden hearted whore, Gullabo is Vijay\u2019s only well-wisher . &nbsp;She chances upon the papers of Vijay\u2019s poems\nwhich his brothers disposed off a scrap. &nbsp;She appreciates his stirring poetry and falls\nin love with him.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">When Vijay learns of\nhis mother\u2019s death he reaches his threshold limit of his tolerance. &nbsp;In a bout of alcohol powered depression he\ndecides to commit suicide on the train tracks. &nbsp;&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">On the way he sees a\nbeggar shivering in the cold . &nbsp;He gives\nhim his coat and proceeds. &nbsp;The beggar\nfollows him but his foot gets caught in the tracks, with a train rushing in. &nbsp;Vijay attempts to save him, &nbsp;but is unable. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">The beggar is killed,\nbut his face and body is badly disfigured. &nbsp;His coat and &nbsp;note in the pocket causes people to believe\nthat it was Vijay who committed suicide.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Gulabo goes to Ghosh\nand gets Vijay\u2019s poems published, by giving up her wealth. &nbsp;Ghosh does so feeling he can exploit the poems\nof a dead poet and make a financial killing out of people\u2019s sentiments. &nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">When Vijay resurrects\nfrom the dead, the people who make money out of his work would rather not see\nhim alive. &nbsp;He is dismissed as a imposter, and humiliated.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; They &nbsp;lock him up in a mental\nasylum, for claiming he the author of his own book.. &nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">I have once got caught in a cloud cover on Table Mountain Capetown. We were stuck there for 4 hours. All the 6 people in our group got separated. &nbsp;While standing we could not even see our own shoes.</span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; line-height: 150%; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-_iCGenMgoII/UUih2M6S3wI/AAAAAAAAgqw/Ktrr_fgff7E/s1600/gyk56.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-_iCGenMgoII/UUih2M6S3wI/AAAAAAAAgqw/Ktrr_fgff7E/s400/gyk56.jpg\" height=\"266\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<span style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;;\"><b><i><span style=\"font-size: small;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">Above: Table&nbsp;</span></span><span style=\"line-height: 24px;\">mountain</span><span style=\"font-size: small;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;of Capetown South Africa-- the cloud cover is called the table cloth</span></span></i></b></span><br />\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">We first went to Kollur\nMookabmika temple in our own car . &nbsp;Outside\nthe temple &nbsp;baby elephant was busy blessing\npeople in return for food and small change. The money the elephant gave the\nmahout. The food like bananas , it polished off. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">How did a temple come\nup in such a desolate ( but beautiful ) spot. &nbsp;It is on the banks of the perennial river\nSauparnika. &nbsp;It is considered &nbsp;one of themost sacred spots in India , with\nlakhs of visitors every year.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; line-height: 150%; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-rt6UX6L5r0w/UUlQK3gVBKI/AAAAAAAAgr4/HQvaYOADOYo/s1600/DFHJK.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-rt6UX6L5r0w/UUlQK3gVBKI/AAAAAAAAgr4/HQvaYOADOYo/s400/DFHJK.jpg\" height=\"481\" width=\"640\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Statistics state that people have been cured of\nuncurable ailments . Childless couples usually come here.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">The temple has a gold\nplated crest and copper roofs ..<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">4000 year ago, Adi Shankaracharya\nmeditated and did penace at Chitramoola cave and Devi appeared before him. He\nrequested the Devi to come with him to Kerala. She agreed, on one condition,\nthat she would follow him and he should never look back to check if she is following.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;It would be a test of faith over senses.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Adi Shankara agreed and\nstarted walking. He could hear the sound of the anklets bells of Devi as she\nwalked behind him. When he reached Kollur , after a 40 mile walk, &nbsp;suddenly the jingle sounds of Devi\u2019s anklets\nstopped.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; line-height: 150%; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-ydue_jsiS8g/UUlP6aW9iiI/AAAAAAAAgro/iwWkUlSZXcg/s1600/sri-adi-shankara-the-goddess.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-ydue_jsiS8g/UUlP6aW9iiI/AAAAAAAAgro/iwWkUlSZXcg/s400/sri-adi-shankara-the-goddess.jpg\" height=\"320\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Adi Shankara became\nsuspicious that Devi has stopped following Him. He turned to check out. &nbsp;Devi was very much behind him, but, since the\nvow was broken, Devi said, \u201cI will not follow you anymore. &nbsp;I will stay here at this spot \u201d.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">That is the\nspot where Kollur Mookambika temple is today. Sankara was saddened by the turn\nof events and begged the forgiveness of the Devi whose heart melted for her\ndevotee and promised that she would present herself at Chottanikkara temple in\nthe mornings and he could meet her there. &nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; line-height: 150%; text-align: center;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; line-height: 150%; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-GezAO3lV08g/UUlQB-_5AFI/AAAAAAAAgr0/b2U6gJ_TIMs/s1600/downloadkkjjuut.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-GezAO3lV08g/UUlQB-_5AFI/AAAAAAAAgr0/b2U6gJ_TIMs/s400/downloadkkjjuut.jpg\" height=\"299\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Only after the morning pooja is over at\nChottanikkara will the temple doors of Mookambika be opened for Darshan and\npooja since the Goddesshas to leave Chottanikkara for Mookambika.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">The Goddess merged with\na huge underground stone &nbsp;of 42\nkilometers radius , with its &nbsp;apex visible,\nlike an iceberg.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; line-height: 150%; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-y-AldvHYts8/UUlPwO500YI/AAAAAAAAgrg/Fd_lyCQIXf0/s1600/imagesjyt.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-y-AldvHYts8/UUlPwO500YI/AAAAAAAAgrg/Fd_lyCQIXf0/s1600/imagesjyt.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; line-height: 150%;\">Adi Shankara made a powerful idol which is the\nreplica of the image of Devi that he witnessed. &nbsp;All the decorations are done on this idol,\nwhile all the offerings are done on the stone which has a golden lining in the\nmiddle. &nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; line-height: 150%;\">Right side of the Golden lining\nrepresents the trinity, Brahma, Vishnu and Shiva and left side represents,\nGoddesses Saraswati, Mahalakshmi, Durga and Kali.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; The lamps are lighted on festive occasions like Navarathri\nand during the Rathotsava. ( chariot festival ) <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; line-height: 150%; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-l0s0ya6Yo9U/UUlRvHwTODI/AAAAAAAAgsY/VdzvTL4AMXM/s1600/DSC02307.JPG\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-l0s0ya6Yo9U/UUlRvHwTODI/AAAAAAAAgsY/VdzvTL4AMXM/s320/DSC02307.JPG\" height=\"320\" width=\"240\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">This Sthambha rests on\na Koorma Peeta ( tortoise seat ) and on this tortoise is a huge elephant upon\nwhich Lord Ganapati idol can be seen facing Goddess Mookambika Devi. The lamps\nare lighted on special festive days. &nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; line-height: 150%; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-zjHT9G6rKnA/UUlR4DQ-80I/AAAAAAAAgsg/guGjmBAraMA/s1600/mkb_pallakku1.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Ganapati\nis the son of Goddess Parvati, who is worshiped as Sri Mookambika. &nbsp;The Mookambika Temple is the only temple that\nis dedicated to goddess Parvathi. &nbsp;The goddess\n&nbsp;is symbolized here as the four armed\ndivine Mother whose upper left hand holds the conch while the right hand holds\nthe scalar discus. &nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; line-height: 150%; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-pYtBZ30234w/UUlPoeKe3CI/AAAAAAAAgrY/PfPP5Ni02Zo/s1600/imagesswdxwxd.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;Lower left hand shows the mystic abhayamudra\nwhile the right hand expresses abheeshta-mudra. The former gives freedom from\nfear and the latter symbol promises fulfillment in life.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">From Mookambika temple\nwe hired a Mahindra jeep and travelled to Kudajadri . The usual nearest 40\nkilometer route was under repair, so we had to take the second best route of 110\nkilometers , which takes 3 hours.&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; line-height: 150%; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-qqpV51inG3c/UUlQwVw9ecI/AAAAAAAAgsI/aziVQa_AeME/s1600/dsc00156-out.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-qqpV51inG3c/UUlQwVw9ecI/AAAAAAAAgsI/aziVQa_AeME/s320/dsc00156-out.jpg\" height=\"298\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; line-height: 150%;\">The\nlast 45 minutes if a steep climb on a raw bumpy with plenty of hairpin bends. &nbsp;This could hardly be called a motorable road. &nbsp;&nbsp;But the\ndriver drove like a possessed manic with his 2 wheel drive jeep bouncing and swaying, like a slow roller coaster. &nbsp;&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; line-height: 150%;\">Sometimes\nthe jeep tilted 40 degrees with all of us holding on for dear life. &nbsp;At one hairpin bend he had to reverse as the\nbend could NOT be navigated in one go. &nbsp;To\nbe frank I never expected something like this.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; After the driver took us up and down safely I\ngave him a handsome bonus.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-TWR5YgJZETM/UUlPNwt_1KI/AAAAAAAAgrQ/d1glGKZUD-Q/s400/saraswathi+temple-kollur1.jpg\" height=\"300\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><i><b><span style=\"color: blue;\">Above Moolasthana, where there is a perenial stone stepped pond full of fishes.</span></b></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">The jeep can only go up to the PWD rest house ( Moolasthana )\nafter which we have to climb about 1.9 kilometers on foot, to reach the apex of\nthe mountain where Sarvajnana peedam or Sankara Peedam is situated..&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">At Moolasthana my wife\ngave offerings to the temple before we set out for the climb. &nbsp;At Moolasthana\nDevi had killed the demon Mookasura, and you can see the 35 feet handle end of\nthe metal trident spear sticking out. &nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; line-height: 150%; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-x2p2TUslcRU/UUlRngCJoZI/AAAAAAAAgsQ/-gjp4e-Fox8/s1600/OAAAABl0MXzeAjru8XpfuKArzq0kcuwPZ3w6W2cjp886Ml5ITUw70P-OMQY1cdXI3QDYqRWtrGSexuDE6MIpTuB6liEAm1T1ULHC7WZykyX_V1YpFOah9SQ8hpZV.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-x2p2TUslcRU/UUlRngCJoZI/AAAAAAAAgsQ/-gjp4e-Fox8/s320/OAAAABl0MXzeAjru8XpfuKArzq0kcuwPZ3w6W2cjp886Ml5ITUw70P-OMQY1cdXI3QDYqRWtrGSexuDE6MIpTuB6liEAm1T1ULHC7WZykyX_V1YpFOah9SQ8hpZV.jpg\" height=\"240\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Indian\nscientists from NITK, Suratkal conducted a test on this spear &nbsp;and found that it was made from traditional\nIndian metallurgical skills. &nbsp;Nobody knows\nthe composition of the alloy yet as the spear has NOT rusted despite being more\nthan 4000 years old.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; line-height: 150%; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-lNvVJas2qRk/UUlPIatP-qI/AAAAAAAAgrI/Jat9SsJyLYI/s1600/mahishasurmardini.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-lNvVJas2qRk/UUlPIatP-qI/AAAAAAAAgrI/Jat9SsJyLYI/s320/mahishasurmardini.jpg\" height=\"320\" width=\"240\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">But it appears to have an angstrom thin oxide veneer which\npassivates the spear exterior, with a protective patina armour.. Otherwise no\nmetal spear can last this long considering the amount of rainfall this place\ngets.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; line-height: 150%; text-align: center;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; line-height: 150%; text-align: center;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; line-height: 150%; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-M_B_QpiBWA8/UUl7w4tUU3I/AAAAAAAAgts/96-MXCvWjn4/s1600/3436812539_0e2f3a273f.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-M_B_QpiBWA8/UUl7w4tUU3I/AAAAAAAAgts/96-MXCvWjn4/s320/3436812539_0e2f3a273f.jpg\" height=\"214\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">The place where devi\nkilled Mookasura is known as \u201cMarana Katte\u201d. The lore is as follows.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Long ago there was this\nfierce demon called Kaumasura , who terrorized all and sundry. So much that mountain\nof &nbsp;Kodachadri became the hiding place\nfor all the gods . Soon the Saptarishis were engaged in prayers and poojas to\nbring about the end of evil demon Kaumasura.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Guru Shukracharya enlightens the demon about\nhis impending death at the hands of a woman. &nbsp;Learning this, Kaumasura performs an austere\npenance to please Lord Shiva. .</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-8qk5Y5lJpZw/UUl96Q0FdYI/AAAAAAAAguE/CzqdKcrEVkA/s1600/imageshtr.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-8qk5Y5lJpZw/UUl96Q0FdYI/AAAAAAAAguE/CzqdKcrEVkA/s400/imageshtr.jpg\" height=\"400\" width=\"299\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Pretty soon the lord pleased with the demon's &nbsp;prayers, appeared before him and asked him to name the boon that he wishes. &nbsp;Vagdevi, the Goddess of speech senses that this could lead to a great disaster\n. So she takes away his power of speech..&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times New Roman, serif; font-size: small;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">The dumb Kaumasura then becomes\nunable to verbalise his wishes and then onwards he was called Mookasura. &nbsp;Mookam means dumb in&nbsp;</span></span><span style=\"font-family: Times New Roman, serif;\"><span style=\"line-height: 24px;\">Sanskrit</span></span><span style=\"font-family: Times New Roman, serif; font-size: small;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;and Malayalam.&nbsp;</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: Times New Roman, serif; font-size: small;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; line-height: 150%; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-b5Caszb0NIk/UUl8j1-OKQI/AAAAAAAAgtw/jy-CvnQ2C8A/s1600/sa14.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-b5Caszb0NIk/UUl8j1-OKQI/AAAAAAAAgtw/jy-CvnQ2C8A/s400/sa14.jpg\" height=\"212\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Soon\nafter, on the request of Kola Rishi, the goddess creates a mystical power by harnessing\nthe individual powers of all the gods who had assembled. &nbsp;This Divine power wages war on Mookasura and kills\nhim with a trident . The place where Devi killed Mookasura is known as\n\"Marana Katte\".<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">However, just before he\ndied, Mookasura repented his misdeeds and, in humble supplication, begged the\nMother Goddess permit him to stay permanently in Kollur. &nbsp;He also asked that his name be remembered\nalong with hers henceforth. &nbsp;It is thus\nthat the deity here is known as Mookambika, the mother of Mooka.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">That is why the temple\nGoddess is worshipped as Sri Saraswathi in the morning , as Sri Lakshmi at noon\nand Sri Durga in the evening. &nbsp;Parents\ntake their young children for writing their first letters and for Goddess\nSaraswati\u2019s &nbsp;( Goddess of learning ) blessings\n.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; line-height: 150%; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-1f3TNYqoi28/UUl7fl8jJGI/AAAAAAAAgtg/VAP20SccEpg/s1600/7.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-1f3TNYqoi28/UUl7fl8jJGI/AAAAAAAAgtg/VAP20SccEpg/s400/7.jpg\" height=\"241\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">From Moolasthana it\ntakes more than one hour to trek 1.8 &nbsp;kilometers, literally an uphill task, and\nreach the top of Kudajadri mountain where the Sarvajnana peedam or Sankarapeedam\nis situated.. Sarvajnapeetam is a rock structure holds only one idol, that of\nAdi Shankaracharya in black stone.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">It is at this Sarvajna\nPeetam ( wholesome wisdom ) , where Adi Shakracharya received the ultimate\nknowledge and dissolved into the universe . The roof from inside has various\nyantras and chakras carved and whole structure forms a Meru.&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; line-height: 150%; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-IYVV1jGdcak/UUl7RbVvL8I/AAAAAAAAgtY/t-GF64clH5M/s1600/meru.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-IYVV1jGdcak/UUl7RbVvL8I/AAAAAAAAgtY/t-GF64clH5M/s320/meru.jpg\" height=\"240\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">On a cloudless day, if you look westwards at\nsunset you can get to see the Arabian Sea. The king cobra, python, tiger,\nleopard, Indian gaur and a variety of birds, including the Malabar pied\nhornbill, inhabit these forest . &nbsp;The\nsides of the mountain drop almost vertically to the impenetrable jungles of\nAmbavana. .<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Enroute to the top is\nthe Ganapathy cave, by taking a small diversion.. &nbsp;There is a Ganapati idol in this cave and a\ntunnel which leads to Mookambika temple at Kollur and also to Chitra moola\ncave. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; line-height: 150%; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-2kHlJ4pxQqg/UUl7J8BI4uI/AAAAAAAAgtQ/K_cab89JDZE/s1600/Kudajadri.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-2kHlJ4pxQqg/UUl7J8BI4uI/AAAAAAAAgtQ/K_cab89JDZE/s400/Kudajadri.jpg\" height=\"386\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">From the peak by a\nsteep treacherous path of 500 metres descent leads to a small cave called Chitramoola, with\na creek and clean and clear water falls , from where the Mookambika temple of\nKollur is visible. You reach a cave at a height of 10 meters., which has\nto be climbed by means of a vertical ladder.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; line-height: 150%; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-fKZ5LR-AnSo/UUl6Q6KWUUI/AAAAAAAAgtA/Ue2OZ4s9jHw/s1600/chitramoola.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-fKZ5LR-AnSo/UUl6Q6KWUUI/AAAAAAAAgtA/Ue2OZ4s9jHw/s400/chitramoola.jpg\" height=\"266\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Chitramoola , one of\nthe most beautiful places of the mountains of Kodachadri and is the spot where\nSri Adi Shankara meditated . &nbsp;This is the place where Goddess Mookambika\nappeared before Shankaracharya . There is a Shivalingam in the cave. &nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; line-height: 150%; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-aoYQUXJ5b9A/UUl7Azq4ipI/AAAAAAAAgtI/OAa9FRgpNaM/s1600/20433_320.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-aoYQUXJ5b9A/UUl7Azq4ipI/AAAAAAAAgtI/OAa9FRgpNaM/s400/20433_320.jpg\" height=\"400\" width=\"339\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">All love to take a shower here in the cool falling\nwaters, which washes off the fatigue . In the rainy season be careful of\nleeches, and it is better to take some powdered salt along.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; line-height: 150%; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-M_B_QpiBWA8/UUl7w4tUU3I/AAAAAAAAgto/wdJLaEaNtRQ/s1600/3436812539_0e2f3a273f.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-M_B_QpiBWA8/UUl7w4tUU3I/AAAAAAAAgto/wdJLaEaNtRQ/s400/3436812539_0e2f3a273f.jpg\" height=\"267\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">The trip is worth it. &nbsp;It gives you a good feeling. &nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">You are convinced that your body and lungs are\nstill healthy and fit. &nbsp;HEALTH IS WEALTH !!<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; , &quot;times&quot; , &quot;freeserif&quot; , serif;\">Horizontal rows add to powers of 2 (i.e., 1, 2, 4, 8, 16, etc.)</span><br /><br /><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times&quot; , &quot;freeserif&quot; , serif;\">Adding any two successive numbers in the diagonal 1-3-6-10-15-21-28\u2026 results in a perfect square (1, 4, 9, 16, etc.)</span><br /><br /><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; This algorithm is known in mathematics as the Sieve of Eratosthenes--inherent in sruti verses of Vedas<br /><br />In mathematics, the sieve of Eratosthenes one of a number of prime number sieves, is a simple, ancient algorithm for finding all prime numbers up to any given limit.<br /><br />It does so by iteratively marking as composite, i.e., not prime, the multiples of each prime, starting with the multiples of 2. The multiples of a given prime are generated starting from that prime, as a sequence of numbers with the same difference, equal to that prime, between consecutive numbers.<br /><br />This is the sieve's key distinction from using trial division to sequentially test each candidate number for divisibility by each prime.<br /><br />MY REVELATIONS NOW JUMP TO&nbsp;<span style=\"color: red; font-size: large;\"><b>52.0 %</b></span><br /><br />capt ajit vadakayil<br />..</span></div>\n</div>\n</li>\n</ol>\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br />\n<div class=\"avatar-image-container\" style=\"float: left; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, FreeSerif, serif; font-size: 16px; margin: 0.2em 0px 0px; max-height: 36px; overflow: hidden; width: 36px;\">\n<img src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-0Gvy5mBcipE/WlAJZNfU3zI/AAAAAAABXsU/wZaBJr4cOoclmnshY0dz6Y3NbokDpLaaACK4BGAYYCw/s35/*\" style=\"border: 1px solid rgb(238, 238, 238); max-width: 36px;\" /></div>\n<div class=\"comment-block\" id=\"c4422559943530061338\" style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, FreeSerif, serif; font-size: 16px; margin-left: 48px; position: relative;\">\n<div class=\"comment-header\" id=\"bc_0_29M\" kind=\"m\" style=\"margin: 0px 0px 8px;\">\n<cite class=\"user blog-author\" style=\"font-style: normal; font-weight: bold;\"><a href=\"https://www.blogger.com/profile/14410812789424637654\" rel=\"nofollow\" style=\"color: #888888; text-decoration-line: none;\">Capt. Such is the effect of this cult, that its leadership's charisma and\nintegrity is not to be questioned.&nbsp; In\nthe Amway business, distributors are taught that there is virtually no other\nlifestyle worthwhile outside of the Amway business.&nbsp; <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">The speeches pound into\nthe heads that a distributor will only be happy when he reaches the Diamond\nlevel- but he will never tell them it is beyond reach. He will never tell you\nhow much time you need to spend to break even, leave alone make a tidy profit.\n.&nbsp; They are told again and again that\nthis is a \"proven system\", and if they just follow it like a recipe\nthey will retire in about 4 years.</span></div>\n<br />\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The Amway dream began\nin 1959 in an old garage , where Jay Van Andel and his friend Richard DeVos\ncreated a multi-level marketing plan. They offered laundry and cleaning\nsupplies to start-up entrepreneurs. </span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">For\nJay and Rich, this was THE American way, thus the name, Amway. </span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-gabvYZfnVEQ/UUId8SgvI6I/AAAAAAAAgjc/97Lw0Uepp1o/s1600/GBL_AA_COFOUNDERS_IMG_1.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"181\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-gabvYZfnVEQ/UUId8SgvI6I/AAAAAAAAgjc/97Lw0Uepp1o/s320/GBL_AA_COFOUNDERS_IMG_1.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Van Andel was born in Grand Rapids, Michigan,\nin 1924. He met Richard DeVos in high school when Van Andel charged DeVos 25\ncents for rides to school in his 1929 Model A Ford, so much for being close\nbuddies. </span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Their first product was\ncalled Frisk, a concentrated organic cleaner developed by a scientist in Ohio.\nDeVos and Van Andel bought the rights to manufacture and distribute Frisk, and\nlater changed the name to LOC (Liquid Organic Cleaner)</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">They went around telling that Multilevel\nmarketing is just a way to remove the average person in the buying and selling\nprocess of a service or product and give the cost of marketing back to the\ncustomer. Oh yeah? The more you buy, the poorer you get but the\n\"richer\" your \"upline\" gets. Their refrain </span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">was the usual bull \"you have to spend it\nto earn it\", \"work now, play later\u201d.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">You were also highly encouraged\nto disassociate yourself from quitters because they will \"try and steal\nyour dream\u201d. So then Amway becomes No.25 among the largest private companies in\nthe U.S. by Forbes in 2012. </span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">How sweet.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Multi level marketing\nbusiness that relies on selling to people you know, then they sell to people\nthey know and on and on. You are given \"gem\" names to represent where\nyou are in the business regarding your sales to further inflate your ego and\ncreate more false security. Ruby &amp; Sapphire's are mid range but the big\ngoal is to make \"Diamond\" and then there is also \"Double fu#ckin\u2019\nDiamond\".<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Upline is the name given to everyone a head of\nyou and \"downline\" is for those beneath you. Steve Van Andel and Dick DeVos succeeded their fathers\nas chairman and president, respectively. Doug Van Andel, another son of Jay's,\nis now president. , &quot;serif&quot;; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: blue; font-size: large;\"><b>On August 6, 2011\nKerala Police sealed the offices of Amway at Kozhikode, Kannur, Kochi,\nKottayam, Thrissur, Kollam and Thiruvananthapuram following <span style=\"background-color: yellow;\">complaints of being\nsold fake dreams.</span></b></span></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The dream sold by the website\nof Amway India offers its members a monthly of Rs. 62,500 if they succeed in\nenrolling 102 members downline of each member with the business model of 6-4-3.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; If the cycle is completed the first member\nwould earn every month Rs. 62,500 without any personal effort, like magic.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; max-width: 36px;\" /></div>\n<div class=\"comment-block\" id=\"c2672388927885150572\" style=\"margin-left: 48px; position: relative;\">\n<div class=\"comment-header\" id=\"bc_0_18M\" kind=\"m\" style=\"margin: 0px 0px 8px;\">\n<cite class=\"user blog-author\" style=\"font-style: normal; font-weight: bold;\"><a href=\"https://www.blogger.com/profile/14410812789424637654\" rel=\"nofollow\" style=\"color: #888888; text-decoration-line: none;\">Capt. Ajit Vadakayil</a></cite><span class=\"icon user blog-author\" style=\"background-image: url(&quot;data:image/png; background-repeat: no-repeat; display: inline-block; font-weight: bold; height: 18px; margin: 0px 0px -4px 6px; width: 18px;\"></span><span class=\"datetime secondary-text\" style=\"margin-left: 6px;\"><a href=\"https://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.com/2018/11/open-letter-to-romila-thapar-from-capt.html?showComment=1541854404047#c2672388927885150572\" rel=\"nofollow\" style=\"color: #888888; text-decoration-line: none;\">November 10, 2018 at 6:23 PM</a></span></div>\n<div class=\"comment-content\" id=\"bc_0_18MC\" style=\"margin-bottom: 8px; text-align: justify;\">\nhttp://www.asianage.com/india/all-india/061118/govt-rbi-row-may-delay-bill-urjit-to-skip-ls-panel-hearing.html<br /><br />QUOTE: owing to URJIT Patel\u2019s absence, the scheduled sitting of the parliamentary standing committee on finance next week has been postponed. This could delay the committee\u2019s finalising its report on the Banning of Unregulated Deposit Schemes Bill 2018. UNQUOTE<br /><br /><span style=\"color: red;\">http://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.com/2013/03/amway-merchants-of-pipe-dreams-capt.html</span><br /><br />IN A PYRAMIDS SCHEME ONLY THE APEX OF THE PYRAMID MAKES MONEY..<br /><br />THE TOP IS USUALLY A JEW..<br /><br />THE LAYER BELOW HIM ARE HIS BENAMI AGENTS.<br /><br />THE JEW MAKES ALL THE MOOLAH SITTING ON HIS KOSHER ASS.<br /><br />As its name indicates, the pyramid scheme is structured like a pyramid.<br /><br />It starts with one JEW ( OR HIS BENAMIFRONT ) - the initial recruiter - who is on top, at the apex of the pyramid. This person recruits a second person, who is required to \"invest\" for instance Rs 10,000 which is paid to the initial recruiter.<br /><br />In order to make his or her money back, the new recruit must recruit more people under him or her, each of whom will also have to invest Rs 10,000. If the recruit gets 10 more people to invest, this person will make Rs 90,000 with just a Rs 10,000 investment.<br /><br />The 10 new people become recruiters and each one is in turn required to enlist an additional 10 people, resulting in a total of 100 more people. Each of those 100 new recruits is also obligated to pay Rs 10,000 to the person who recruited him or her; recruiters get a profit of all of the money received minus the initial Rs 10,000 paid to the person who recruited them.<br /><br />The process continues until the base of the pyramid is no longer strong enough to support the upper structure (meaning there are no more fools to recruit)<br /><br />People are deceived into believing that by giving money they will make more money (\"with an investment of just Rs 10,000, you will receive Rs 90,000 in return\"). But no wealth has been created; no product has been sold; no investment has been made; and no service has been provided.<br /><br />It becomes easy when the Pyramid Schemers pay the first batch of people, this is because they now have vocal ambassadors and witnesses who have been paid and hence can convince people that scheme is a legitimate one. The fraud lies in the fact that it is impossible for the cycle to sustain itself, so people will lose their money somewhere down the line.<br /><br />Those who are most vulnerable are those towards the bottom of the pyramid, where it becomes impossible to recruit the number of people required to pay off the previous layer of recruiters.<br /><br />It is estimated that 94 % of people who get involved in a pyramid scheme will lose their money.<br /><br />Because people are attracted to the idea of making a quick buck with very little effort, many different forms of disguised pyramid schemes have succeeded in fooling people. Despite the illusion of legality presented by these revamped schemes, they are still illegal.<br /><br />Legal multi-level marketing (MLM) , involves being recruited in order to sell a product or service that actually has some inherent value. As a recruit, you can make a profit from the sales of the product or service, so you don't necessarily have to recruit more salespeople below you.<br /><br />CONTINUED TO 2--</div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"comment-replies\" id=\"bc_0_18BR\" style=\"margin-left: 36px; margin-top: 1em;\">\n<span id=\"bc_0_18b+seedDx7aD\" kind=\"d\"><div class=\"comment-thread inline-thread\" id=\"bc_0_17T\" kind=\"t\" style=\"background-color: #eeeeee; margin: 8px 0px; padding: 0.5em 1em;\" t=\"0\" u=\"0\">\n<span class=\"thread-toggle thread-expanded\" id=\"bc_0_17TT\" kind=\"g\" style=\"cursor: pointer; display: inline-block;\"><span class=\"thread-count\" id=\"bc_0_17TN\"><div class=\"thread-dropContainer thread-expanded\" id=\"bc_0_17TD\">\n<span class=\"thread-drop\"></span></div>\n</span></span><ol class=\"thread-chrome thread-expanded\" id=\"bc_0_17TC\" style=\"list-style-type: none; padding: 0px;\">\n<li class=\"comment\" id=\"bc_0_17B\" kind=\"b\" style=\"border-bottom: 0px; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 16px 0px 0px;\"><div class=\"avatar-image-container\" style=\"float: left; margin: 0.2em 0px 0px; max-height: 36px; overflow: hidden; width: 36px;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"comment-block\" id=\"c8011528766040904900\" style=\"margin-left: 48px; position: relative;\">\n<div class=\"comment-header\" id=\"bc_0_17M\" kind=\"m\" style=\"margin: 0px 0px 8px;\">\n<cite class=\"user blog-author\" style=\"font-style: normal; font-weight: bold;\"><a href=\"https://www.blogger.com/profile/14410812789424637654\" rel=\"nofollow\" style=\"color: #888888; text-decoration-line: none;\">Capt. Ajit Vadakayil</a></cite><span class=\"icon user blog-author\" style=\"background-image: url(&quot;data:image/png; background-repeat: no-repeat; display: inline-block; font-weight: bold; height: 18px; margin: 0px 0px -4px 6px; width: 18px;\"></span><span class=\"datetime secondary-text\" style=\"margin-left: 6px;\"><a href=\"https://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.com/2018/11/open-letter-to-romila-thapar-from-capt.html?showComment=1541854436814#c8011528766040904900\" rel=\"nofollow\" style=\"color: #888888; text-decoration-line: none;\">November 10, 2018 at 6:23 PM</a></span></div>\n<div class=\"comment-content\" id=\"bc_0_17MC\" style=\"margin-bottom: 8px; text-align: justify;\">\nCONTINUED FROM 1-<br /><br />And while you may be encouraged to recruit other salespeople whose sales would give you more profit, you can stick to just selling the product directly to the consumer if you choose.<br /><br />Ponzi Schemes-- Named after Charles Ponzi, who ran such a plot from 1919-1920, the Ponzi scheme is a fraudulent investment plan. It is not necessarily a pyramid, which is hierarchical.<br /><br />In a Ponzi scheme, there is one person who takes people's money as an \"investment\" and does not necessarily tell them how their returns will be generated.<br /><br />As such, the people's return on investment could be generated by anything; it could come from money taken from new investors - which means new investors essentially pay off the old investors<br /><br />They usually tell ignorant Kenyans that they invest in teak trees on banks of the river Nile , offshore trade and have business in tax free Havens. . This is the most difficult type to identify; this is because they hire smart marketers and know how to network with opinion leaders in any society so as to earn the confidence of the locals.<br /><br />capt ajit vadakayil<br />..</div>\n</div>\n</li>\n</ol>\n</div>\n</span></div>\n</li>\n</ol>\n<span style=\"color: blue;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"color: blue;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"color: blue;\">Grace and peace!</span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<object class=\"BLOGGER-youtube-video\" classid=\"clsid:D27CDB6E-AE6D-11cf-96B8-444553540000\" codebase=\"http://download.macromedia.com/pub/shockwave/cabs/flash/swflash.cab#version=6,0,40,0\" data-thumbnail-src=\"http://img.youtube.com/vi/lb17gpRSQU8/0.jpg\" height=\"266\" width=\"320\"><param name=\"movie\" value=\"http://youtube.googleapis.com/v/lb17gpRSQU8&source=uds\" /><param name=\"bgcolor\" value=\"#FFFFFF\" /><param name=\"allowFullScreen\" value=\"true\" /><embed width=\"320\" height=\"266\"  src=\"http://youtube.googleapis.com/v/lb17gpRSQU8&source=uds\" type=\"application/x-shockwave-flash\" allowfullscreen=\"true\"></embed></object></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<o:p></o:p></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-itWPy7qxzvM/UUIe3Np-GlI/AAAAAAAAgj8/Aldq-gk98_E/s1600/BB.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-itWPy7qxzvM/UUIe3Np-GlI/AAAAAAAAgj8/Aldq-gk98_E/s1600/BB.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nCAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL<br />\n..<br />\n<br /></div>\n</div>\n</div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n</div>\n", "author": {"id": "14410812789424637654", "displayName": "Capt. Teach him to\nscoff at cynics and to beware of too much sweetness.<o:p></o:p></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><i>Teach him to sell his\nbrawn and brain to the highest bidders; but never to put a price tag on his\nheart and soul.<o:p></o:p></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><i>Teach him to close his\nears to a howling mob\u2026 and to stand and fight if he thinks he\u2019s right.<o:p></o:p></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><i>Treat him gently; but\ndo not cuddle him because only the test of fire makes fine steel.<o:p></o:p></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><i>Let him have the\ncourage to be impatient, let him have the patience to be brave. Teach him\nalways to have sublime faith in himself because then he will always have\nsublime faith in mankind.</i></span><i style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;</i></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><i>This is a big order;\nbut see what you can do. He is such a fine little fellow, my son.<o:p></o:p></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><i>Abraham Lincoln.</i><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">People who judge this\npost must know that I am 3 in 1 on the ships I command -- judge, jury and\npolice.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><b style=\"background-color: yellow;\">WE ARE ALL INHERENTLY\nGOOD PEOPLE&nbsp;</b> ( leave out the criminal gene\nholders ).<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">When you make a\njudgement ask yourself certain questions. &nbsp;Propel yourself back in time, imagine you are\nnow 22 years old. &nbsp;A white woman begged\nyou to accompany here on a tour. font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Although the\nreal glycerin is sweet in taste, added with beer may cause a bitter taste at\nthe end. </span><span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; line-height: 150%;\">Beer comprises of 93%\nwater. It is made from malted barley, cereals, hops, yeast and water. Carbohydrates\nin the beer are in liquid form which means they can be assimilated quickly by\nthe body. It is a low alcohol beverage (4.5%) in comparison with wine (12%) and\nspirits such as vodka or whisky (45%).&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">This means less pure alcohol entering\nthe body. 100ml of a 5 per cent lager contained 43 calories, compared to the 84\ncalories of the same quantity of a 12 per cent white wine.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">The digestive system is not taxed. It is an effective\naperitif . The only natural drinks with fewer calories than beer are plain tea,\nblack coffee and water.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Moderate drinkers live\nlonger and better than drunks or teetotalers. Beer is perfect for moderate\ndrinking because of its lower alcohol content and larger volume compared with\nwine or spirits.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Beer contains over 30\ndifferent minerals that come from malted barley . Beer contains significant\namounts of nutrients, including magnesium, selenium, potassium, phosphorus,\nbiotin and chromium.&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; It is\npreventive against heart disease and against the formation of kidney stones and\nurinary tract. The low sodium content of beer means that it is low in salt and\nit has a diuretic effect.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">The high content of minerals, particularly potassium\nand magnesium, regulates electrolyte balance and ensures trouble-free cellular\nfunctionality.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Beer acts as a diuretic\nbecause it is low in sodium and high in potassium, which helps cleanse the\nbody. &nbsp;It has high levels of B vitamins,\nparticularly folic acid, which is believed to help prevent heart attacks. Sodium is known as a cation because it has more\nprotons than electrons and carries a positive charge. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">When there is ample\npotassium inside of your cells and sodium outside of your cells, proper cell\nsignaling from your nervous system can take place.&nbsp;&nbsp; Magnesium plays a large role in the\nutilization of potassium; it modulates a primary potassium transport system in\nand out of individual cells, and is crucial in preventing intracellular\npotassium loss.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Magnesium provides for optimum utilization of potassium and\nprotects stores of potassium from depletion. font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">The heart is NOT an\n\"organ,\" but is actually a \"muscle.\" &nbsp;In fact, it's the hardest working muscle in\nour body. &nbsp;Every 24 hours our hearts beat\nmore than a lakh times and circulates 9000 litres of blood. The highest\nconcentration of magnesium in our body is in the heart ventricles, which are\nthe muscles that \"pump\" all that blood. &nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Muscle energy in our body is solely in the\nform of Mg2-ATP (Magnesium-adenosine triphosphate). &nbsp;Our heart cells (and every cell in our body)\nmust have magnesium present in plentiful amounts to create and metabolize the\nATP necessary to run all of the cell's activities. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">When electrolyte\nimbalance becomes great enough, the cell no longer has the ability to produce\nATP. &nbsp;ATP is primarily dependent on\nmagnesium. &nbsp;So, cell death - cardiac\nnecrosis is the result of a systemic shortage of magnesium. Heart muscle cell\ndeath is followed by inflammation in order to clean up the debris from dying\ncells followed by fibrosis/calcification as the whole area contracts and scars\ndown in order to isolate, repair and minimize the damage.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Chronic stress causes\nmagnesium loss, which then leads to cell death. The cellular influx of excess,\nunregulated calcium accelerates this process. &nbsp;If magnesium isn't available, the mineral ion\nchannels in cells are left wide open and calcium floods in.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Any cell unable to\ncreate proper levels of energy becomes diseased and dies, and this is\nespecially true of heart muscles cells. \"Stress,\" in all its many\nforms leads to magnesium use, and if not curtailed, magnesium loss. An\naccelerated MBR (Magnesium Burn Rate) leads to electrolyte dysfunction, which\nresults in imbalances of our key minerals. The chronic loss of magnesium leads\nto a relentless increase of sodium and calcium which ultimately becomes the\ngreatest form of cellular \"Stress.\"<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Unregulated calcium is\nbad for you. And how do we create a condition of calcium excess? Human\nbiochemistry strongly favors holding onto as much calcium as possible. However,\nmagnesium is flushed out through the urine or bowels when the body is under\nstress .</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">People with high calcium and low levels of magnesium can suffer sudden\ndeath heart attacks due to electrical imbalance without having significant\ncoronary artery calcification. &nbsp;</span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n</div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Excess calcium reduces\nmagnesium. &nbsp;Calcium and magnesium work\ntogether in muscle contraction and relaxation. &nbsp;If magnesium isn't available, the mineral ion\nchannels in cells are left wide open and calcium floods in leading to it's\ncalcification. Loss of magnesium leads to a relentless increase of sodium and\ncalcium which ultimately becomes the greatest form of cellular \"Stress\u201d. &nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Dominance of calcium over magnesium produces\nsymptoms of muscle spasm. Migraines, eyelid twitch, heart flutters, back aches,\npremenstrual tension, leg cramps and constipation are all linked to calcium\noverload. &nbsp;Excessive calcium may also\nresult in kidney stones and heart valve calcifications. In a diet lacking essential minerals and\nvitamins, molecules in the body lose electrons and become free radicals. These\nfree radicals attack healthy cells to take back electrons damaging even more cells.\nAs the cell\u2019s efficiency degenerates in long term, the genetic material in the\ncell gets damaged or changes, its processes go wrong and produce mutations.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Magnesium deficiency can lead directly to cancer. While calcium is not used in\nmany enzymes in the body, magnesium is a component of thousands of enzyme. Magnesium\nis essential for thousands of enzymes in the body and may be said to represent\nenzyme strength, while calcium represents structural strength or bone strength.\n.&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">In electrical terms, calcium\nrepresents a compressive pressure or voltage.&nbsp;\nMagnesium is tensive and more about amperage or intensity.&nbsp; Ohm\u2019s law and Joule\u2019s law apply here.&nbsp; For example, Joule\u2019s law states that voltage\nmultiplied by amps = power or watts.&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Both Calcium and Magnesium are divalent cations, both form hard\ncompounds, and both have a mainly calming effect on the body, although\nmagnesium is needed for energy production, as well.
