The pancreas then produces more insulin to\nnormalize blood sugar. The end result of chronic stress is exhausted adrenal\nglands and an exhausted pancreas.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-cOJHL7FJC4U/UTnR8R7a9OI/AAAAAAAAgZY/wI1KzaB80Ts/s1600/imagesUKUYKTG.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-cOJHL7FJC4U/UTnR8R7a9OI/AAAAAAAAgZY/wI1KzaB80Ts/s1600/imagesUKUYKTG.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">A healthy cell has a\nbeautiful, fluid phospholipids membrane around it which allow nutrients,\nelectrolytes and waste matter to move freely in and out of the cell.</span> &nbsp;<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">The core of this healing in terms\nof sodium/potassium and calcium/magnesium balances is all about energy. Our\npolarity gives us life - it is an electrical charge, an electrical current. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">You can take this\npolarity right down to its expression at cellular level.&nbsp; Minerals have different charges and the\npolarity is a function of the interaction between the four electrolytes: sodium\nand potassium (male and female) and between calcium (male charge, like sodium)\nand magnesium (female charge, like potassium).<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Vertigo is caused by\ncalcium carbonate crystals forming in the inner ear. Minerals come out of\nsolution when there is not enough liquid to keep them dissolved. There is not\nenough liquid because the body's cells are not retaining water properly.\nMagnesium regulates water in cells.</span> <span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">To cure vertigo, drink\nmore water and take magnesium. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-HYMJqeQwhiY/UTnRn2ol-MI/AAAAAAAAgZQ/ujBxdoIfdZ8/s1600/MJYRD.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-HYMJqeQwhiY/UTnRn2ol-MI/AAAAAAAAgZQ/ujBxdoIfdZ8/s1600/MJYRD.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">In Ayurveda we just\ndrink coconut water for vertigo.</span> <span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">The balancing mechanism\nin your ears is like the power steering system in your car. It relies on fluid.\nWhen you have vertigo, you have a \"leak\" in your \"power steering\nsystem\". You need to replenish the fluids in it. You can't pour water into\nthe inner ear like you can your car, so you have to re-hydrate or over-hydrate\nevery cell in your body to get the extra fluid up to your ears.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Since 99% of magnesium\nresides inside living cells, blood serum levels are not a good indicator of\nmagnesium deficiency. &nbsp;Ionized magnesium\ntesting is the only effective way of diagnosing accurate magnesium levels in\nthe body.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">A hormone produced in\nthe adrenal glands, aldosterone, plays a role in stimulating the kidneys\u2019\nretention of sodium.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">The adrenal glands also\nproduce a stress hormone, cortisol. The area of the brain that recognizes\nstress is not very sophisticated. It knows only one of two things. Either\nyou\u2019re sitting in peace or a black mamba is chasing you. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Exercising, riding a\nroller coaster, being happy, being sad or anytime you are not relaxed is\ninterpreted as stress. This will trigger a chain reaction that will increase\ncortisol. That same chain reaction will cause a slight increase in aldosterone.\nThe increased aldosterone retains more sodium and dumps more potassium. Sodium\nwill increase the retention of water. The net result is an increase in blood\npressure.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-6twYNOY-GyU/UTnQtJFcDfI/AAAAAAAAgZA/jgcz8_BExOI/s1600/heshetu.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"214\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-6twYNOY-GyU/UTnQtJFcDfI/AAAAAAAAgZA/jgcz8_BExOI/s320/heshetu.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">That would be a good thing if you\u2019re running away from the black\nfu#kin\u2019 mamba .&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">It is not so cool for an office worker.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-size: large;\"><b>By, the way, beer has plenty of Magnesium and Potassium. It gave me a kick to convert fear into excitement, flight\nto fight.<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; There was never a Lok Sabha or a Rajya Sabha on\nmy ship. &nbsp;&nbsp;Yet, I brainstormed frequently and got valuable feedback.<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">My shore bosses never\ndared to tell me from ashore \" CAPTAIN HARD-A-PORT! \" . They did this\nto other Captains , never me.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">My shore bosses whom I liked ,\nbecause they were clean hearted , I spared . &nbsp;The rest of the black hearted knaves , I\nconverted into their own worst enemies, for they deserved it. &nbsp;I just made them jealous.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; People whose jealousy can be kindled are insecure\nneurotics.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Let me put this in most\nlucid terms, meant for a layman . <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">What do you mean by\nkindling jealousy ? &nbsp;If you are not good\nenough you can be burnt very badly . Basically I am a non-conformist who plays better to a hostile crowd. &nbsp;I love to hit consecutive sixes into hostile raging faces.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; line-height: 150%;\">Three and a half\ndecades ago, as &nbsp;young men, we were all\nstanding in line to enter the examination hall at Mumbai MMD, for the First Mate's\nexam. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">One of my long lost\nfriends, &nbsp;shouted out from behind the\nlong line ( i was in front )--\" Ajit , well prepared?\"<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">And this made me very\nunpopular with the dumbos and the paranoids in line , some of whom who were\ngiving their 3rd and 4th shots. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Now after giving this corny\ndialogue , If I fail, you can very well imagine my condition, for we all stayed\ntogether at the Seamen\u2019s club at Ballard Estate. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Now I am rising above myself,\nto explain what jealousy is.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; line-height: 150%; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-u78MoOINDyg/UTAyrcdRtjI/AAAAAAAAgNg/Pw5tx_9qiv0/s1600/imageshjtk.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-u78MoOINDyg/UTAyrcdRtjI/AAAAAAAAgNg/Pw5tx_9qiv0/s1600/imageshjtk.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Let me digress briefly to<b><span style=\"color: blue;\">\n\u201cdog eat dog\u201d office politics</span></b> . It is purely based on jealousy. &nbsp;Jealousy is, &nbsp;the worst of all faults as it makes a victim\nof both parties. It is not love that is blind, but jealousy.<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-RjCpFGwWMRQ/UTA0BWveVDI/AAAAAAAAgNs/9slv6lBEiw4/s1600/imagesfrehrh.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"320\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-RjCpFGwWMRQ/UTA0BWveVDI/AAAAAAAAgNs/9slv6lBEiw4/s320/imagesfrehrh.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; line-height: 150%;\">Knowledge of human\nnature and even style is the corner stone of political education. &nbsp;Recognize tactics used on you.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Power does not come\nwith position of authority. &nbsp;Sometimes a\nslave could be more powerful than the great almighty Caesar . &nbsp;Having said that be aware that knowledge is\npower\u2014 be respected and valued at all levels .<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Be confident. Every power\nplay attacker enjoys seeing fear in the victim. It is a valuable skill to know\nwhen to yield. Keep your emotions under a leash even when you are outraged, but\ndon\u2019t allow yourself to be the scapegoat for someone else\u2019s mistakes.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Keep away from vicious\nsmear campaigns. Do not encourage lying and deception. You will be judged by\nyour communication styles\u2014if you are defensive all the time\u2014you give yourself\naway.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-_RlMeqeX_q0/UTDy66t4I1I/AAAAAAAAgQs/DXR3EHUtrRw/s1600/imagesngfgnt.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-_RlMeqeX_q0/UTDy66t4I1I/AAAAAAAAgQs/DXR3EHUtrRw/s1600/imagesngfgnt.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Be aware , stay focused\nand continue being the team player who will share man of the match awards. To\nstay focused you need to know the larger picture. &nbsp;Do not use the larger picture as a convenient\nexit route. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">In a shore office (\nunlike a ship ) do not tell anyone anything that can be used against you\u2014don\u2019t\nlet go too much even over a Saturday night beer session with buddies who may be\nopportunists \u2014don\u2019t even pass on rumors or share negative career experiences. &nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Be a friend on matters that do not involve the\noffice and an employee on issues that involve your career prospects. There is\nno need to prove your friendship at the expense of compromising your values.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">The truth is without\nengaging in some sort of political activity or trying to develop followers ,\nyour career will stagnate. &nbsp;This is why\nold blunt seadogs , like yours truly, who are not limelight oriented are\nmisfits ashore.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Do favors and help\nothers out. Even asking for help creates bonding ( what a paradox!).<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Know your power\u2014unleash\nit only when necessary at the right time.. Control impulses and rushes of\nblood.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: magenta; There must be an atmosphere of \u201cwe\u2019re\nall in this together.\u201d <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/--I2jnLdEGA8/UTDkxwyF1WI/AAAAAAAAgPs/RZuS0kq4GAU/s1600/dfeq.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"258\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/--I2jnLdEGA8/UTDkxwyF1WI/AAAAAAAAgPs/RZuS0kq4GAU/s400/dfeq.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Women with a high level\nof intrasexual competition are more jealous if the rival is a woman who is more\nattractive and more envious if this rival is more powerful .<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Happiness is a victory\nlap\u2014so solve problems, talk big ( like you know who ), keep the colour in your\ncheek and the glint in your eye. Be yourself, and have good friends who accept\nyou as you are.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Laughing and crying are\nsigns of relief valve lifting on the overstrung\u2014JUST SMILE<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Here is some wisdom--- Champions\nand heroes who challenge themselves have the knowledge, talent, skill ,\nattitude and determination to easily handle the lifetime ahead of them\u2014it is a\npiece of cake.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Can you name one\ncountry who is burning with jealousy? It comforts them, it soothes their worries, and\nfinally it rots their souls, allowing them to justify their meanness and their\ngreed, &nbsp;until they believe these to be virtues.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span><span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; One by one they will\nreveal all her faults.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">He that is jealous is\nnot in love. &nbsp;Jealousy is bred in doubts.\n&nbsp;When those doubts change into\ncertainties, then the passion either ceases or turns absolute madness. &nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">True love is a unique\ncondition where the happiness of the one you love is essential to your own. Love\nlooks through a telescope and envy, through a microscope. &nbsp;When jealous behavior goes completely haywire,\nit can erupt into aggression and possibly turn violent. . <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-mg44-pLuwpQ/UTDylzyCw6I/AAAAAAAAgQc/m31hTUELazM/s1600/imageshttyrd.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-mg44-pLuwpQ/UTDylzyCw6I/AAAAAAAAgQc/m31hTUELazM/s1600/imageshttyrd.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">It may be perfectly\nnormal to feel brief pangs of jealously in response to a perceived threat, say\nif your girl goes to a strip club with a group of friends. Or your wife wears\nmini skirt and sits with her legs splayed for the benefit of a handsome guy whose\neyes are transfixed you know where.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">If a husband suspects\nanother man is flirting with his wife, healthy feelings of jealously will &nbsp;surface. He accepts them as a reminder of how\nmuch he cares for his wife and is quick to let them go because this relationship\nis based on mutual trust. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Jealousy is the result\nor fear of losing your girl to another. &nbsp;In romantic relationships, both men and women\ncontinue to check out other men and women. &nbsp;It's biologically driven and it's natural. However,\n&nbsp;it does not mean that the person wants\nto leave the relationship. &nbsp;It is, for\nmost people, about appreciating the opposite sex human form and not about a\nroaming eye. &nbsp;Touching is taboo, but\njealousy makes looking also taboo.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">On a ship if you have a\nbeer with a buddy daily, &nbsp;and one fine\nday you wait for him and see him having a drink with someone else without\ntelling you, &nbsp;you are bound to feel the\npangs of jealousy.<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/--iO8Fvhfrx0/UTDyYCn1S0I/AAAAAAAAgQU/dSx_vsltIuA/s1600/imagesbjuy.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"259\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/--iO8Fvhfrx0/UTDyYCn1S0I/AAAAAAAAgQU/dSx_vsltIuA/s320/imagesbjuy.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Normal jealousy in a\nrelationship generally stems from a place of love and commitment. &nbsp;When jealously gets out of control, it becomes\ninjurious to both parties involved. Cultivate an attitude of\ngratitude. &nbsp;Only fools live in the past\nor carry envy to the present.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">A couple of days ago, I\nsaw a National Games Taekwondo Championship recording on TV, which was held in the Calicut\nIndoor stadium.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">That sent me down\nmemory lane.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">When I went to the\nswimming pool in Calicut I saw the gym coach and the pool coach about to ride\noff into the sunset on a bike. &nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">So I asked them , what\nis the tearing fu#ckin' hurry?<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Well they just received\nthe news that the UNOFFICIAL championship has just started. &nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">After the results are announced , and if the\nsilver medalist or the bronze medalist feels short changed , due to partial\njudges ( which happens every single time ) then after the trophy ceremony, they\nsettle it out again\u2014this time for real , where real blood flows, and nobody stops\na fight , till one man is down . &nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">And\nsometimes this changes into an all-out FREE FOR ALL brawl . They coaches said that they had\nwitnessed it , the previous two years \u2013 as they rode off .<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">The Calicut indoor\nstadium is attached to the main Calicut Corporation Soccer stadium.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Two decades back I was\na regular at the tennis clay court with my elder son, who was just 6 years old. He\nused to play well and then he lost interest. &nbsp;I guess I pushed him too hard, as a\nfather-coach . This is what happens when play becomes work , and the joy of\nplaying a game is lost. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">The tennis coach was my\ngood friend and he used to introduce me to the National SAI coaches who stayed\nwith their family in the Calicut Indoor stadium complex. &nbsp;And I used to give them fancy baseball caps,\nwhich I bought from USA. &nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">So one day ,\nthe national Table Tennis coach allowed me to play with the National men\u2019s\nchampion. Rather he ordered the champion to play with me , and I got beaten\n21-4. &nbsp;Just one single game.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Then after a couple of\ndays , I wrangled a TT match with the National women\u2019s champion. &nbsp;She won the first game 21-8. &nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">In the second game ,the score was 15-15 , when\nmy tennis coach friend shouted from the side lines \u201c Ajit , what is the score?\u201d\n\u2013 and then she reeled off 6 points in a row and I lost 21-15.<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">After the match the\ntennis coach conveyed to me over a drink , that he has been categorically told\nby the National TT coach Mr Agarwal, that I can never ever play with his\nstudents.&nbsp; Apparently my game is weird ,\nhaving no smash, only ball control and googly spin , and I had totally\ndemoralized the women\u2019s champion. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Twice her bat missed the ball totally, while making &nbsp;top spin full blooded smashes -- &nbsp;which can be very\nembarrassing, even for a novice.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">It seems she used to beat the\nmen\u2019s champion sometimes , and there was NO reason for her to be 15-15 with me. &nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: large; line-height: 150%;\">She and her coach never heard of the MAGNUS EFFECT.</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: large; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"></span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<a href=\"http://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.in/2013/04/swinging-cricket-ball-curving-soccer.html\">http://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.in/2013/04/swinging-cricket-ball-curving-soccer.html</a><o:p></o:p></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: red; font-size: large;\"><b>But then this is what\ncoaching is all about . You have to play to the weaknesses of the opponent. </b></span><span style=\"font-size: small;\"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">The Tennis coach ( we\ncalled him Siddettan ) is now dead. &nbsp;May his soul rests in peace . He was an educated man, and spoke very good\nEnglish , with a good accent , unlike the typical Malayali English accent. &nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">I could have a good intelligent conversation\nwith him. He had hundreds of National Geographic magazines, to which he\nsubscribed . &nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">He died a bachelor . &nbsp;A few weeks before he passed away, we met over a couple of drinks . He told me that\nhe never had sex with a woman, and he often wondered how it would be. &nbsp;Poor guy was the eldest &nbsp;and he has three younger sisters to marry off\n, and it did NOT happen . A sort of domino effect . His 3 sisters were &nbsp;spinsters too. &nbsp;I never asked him why? &nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">One day he confessed that the only time of the\nday he really enjoys, &nbsp;is when he takes out out his\nbottle of whisky from his cupboard and he pours the liquid into his glass.&nbsp; And he used to pour it slow in silence so\nthat he can hear the gurgle and splash of the liquid. And then he used to go to\nsleep thinking about this sweet noise which would happen again the next day. <o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Just to show how life dishes out a raw deal to good people.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">As I said, the main soccer stadium\nis attached to the Indoor stadium or rather vice versa. &nbsp;As a young boy while studying in school , our\nmost exciting period was when the football season started. &nbsp;Our Calicut stadium hosted the Sait Nagjee\nFootball Tournament. &nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-VElxo-Au_HY/USqJtUKQRHI/AAAAAAAAgBQ/YaLkHsha2bs/s1600/images.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"427\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-VElxo-Au_HY/USqJtUKQRHI/AAAAAAAAgBQ/YaLkHsha2bs/s640/images.jpg\" width=\"640\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">The stadium was walking\ndistance from my &nbsp;home. We had a big neighborhood gang of more than 20 young boys. The galleries those days were made of bamboo. &nbsp;Initially our main interest was to go under\nthe stadium bamboo galleries while the match is in progress and forage for empty\ncigarette packets .&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-q_8YtBZOSvU/USqPT43_FdI/AAAAAAAAgCY/AWcBskwk2CU/s1600/1369838429_c7edeb8903.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"274\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-q_8YtBZOSvU/USqPT43_FdI/AAAAAAAAgCY/AWcBskwk2CU/s640/1369838429_c7edeb8903.jpg\" width=\"640\" /></a></div>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">People used to drop the empty packets down.&nbsp; We used to flatten the packet covers of\nScissors, Passing Show, Charminar , Wills brands and take it home. &nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">These were our playing\nchips during outdoor games and gambling chips during the rains , when we were\nconfined indoors.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">The Indoor game when it rained was pretty simple and straight\nforward. &nbsp;A ten paise coin would be\nflipped and the question would come \u201chead or tails?\u201d . I remember in vernacular\nit used to be \u201cGuru or Chapa?\u201d ( or was it bhuru? ) .&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">And then we used to place our bets .<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">The outdoor game was\nquite exciting. A circle would be drawn on the ground and we placed our bets,\nlike cards . &nbsp;A pile would be made and\nkept in the circle. Then we used to go about 30 feet away and fling a flat piece\nof tile , about 3 inch square and half inch thick towards the circle. &nbsp;The child whose tile was closest to the circle\nwould be allowed the first chance of knocking the pile of flattened cigarette\npackets, and put it out of the circle. And then all these packet chips outside the\ncircle would be his. &nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">What a splendid game!&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">We\nspend hundreds of happy hours playing this game. And then we used to run home\nat sunset , count our chips stash it away in our <i>kijoris</i> and feel very proud , if we had a positive flow . &nbsp;Often when a neighbor friend came to visit ,\nhis first request would be \u201c Can you show me your packs!\u201d.<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">And then on seeing a good heap, he would say WOW!-- &nbsp;and my little chest would swell with pride!</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Then as we got older,\nwe started enjoying the soccer tournaments. &nbsp;We used to be so excited that we used to hop\nand skip all the way to the stadium. The atmosphere there would be electrifying\n, especially on Sundays and Saturdays. The best games were reserved for those\ndays. &nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">One day I saw my uncle\n, who stayed 25 kilometers away . And when I told my father , he remarked \u201cHe\nhas a season ticket and he never misses a match \u201c. There were people from neighboring\ndistricts , who used to travel upto 80 miles to see a soccer club game.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;;\"><span style=\"background-color: yellow; font-size: large;\"><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\">Such\nwas the soccer craze in Calicut. Recently Maradona had come to Kannur , my wife's place. Good players were hero&nbsp;</span><span style=\"line-height: 24px;\">worshiped</span></span><span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"background-color: yellow; font-size: large;\">.</span><o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; Finding himself in a terrible financial crisis, he took up a\njob as a private security guard for peanuts. After he married off his daughter\nhe fell into debt, and then he had an accident which made things worse. Today\nhe is a psychological wreck.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-p84wbyueJjo/USqI7E-rdhI/AAAAAAAAgAw/-PmcLc3EPwQ/s1600/main-qimg-a3fee9068bf40520f905a486708a448d.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"395\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-p84wbyueJjo/USqI7E-rdhI/AAAAAAAAgAw/-PmcLc3EPwQ/s640/main-qimg-a3fee9068bf40520f905a486708a448d.jpg\" width=\"640\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">People who recognize him as a past champion who\nwore the Indian Soccer Jersey , tell him to keep the change , which cuts him\nup.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">He even went and met YSR the CM of Andhra Pradesh with his wife Devaki. &nbsp;It was no use and YSR would care for him only\nif he converted to Christianity. Imagine a proud Gorkha having to face this choice and changing his name from Bir Bahadur ( bravest of the brave ) to some Tom, Dick or Prick..<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">You must know that when\nthe media highlighted Bahadur's plight, relief came from Sunil Gavaskar's\nCHAMPS Foundation. &nbsp;After I heard of this, my opinion of Sunil Gavaskar changed and my respect for him has gone up. I had\nnever respected him as a selfish cricketer.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Sometimes Bir Bahadur enjoys\npride of place in VIP enclosures at major football events.
